# SCBot

A bot to suMMarize the [Snap Chat Political Ads Library](https://www.snap.com/en-US/political-ads).

Source and summarized data in CSV format: [/SCData](https://github.com/MassMove/SCBot/tree/master/SCData).

Last run: 2023-04-20.

Last run: 2023-04-20.
